  2565	          qErrors.push(error);
  2566	        }
  2567	      }

  2569	    }

  2574	  }
  2575	  private collectErrors(qErrors: Array<SurveyError>, context: ValidationContext): void {
  2576	    this.onCheckForErrors(qErrors, context.isOnValueChanged, context.fireCallback);
  2577	    if (qErrors.length > 0 || !this.canRunValidators(context.isOnValueChanged)) return;
  2578	    const errors = this.runValidators(context);
  2579	    if (errors.length > 0) {
  2580	      //validators may change the question value.
  2581	      qErrors.length = 0;
  2582	      for (var i = 0; i < errors.length; i++) {
  2583	        qErrors.push(errors[i]);
  2584	      }
  2585	    }
  2586	  }

  2598	      if (!!text) {
  2599	        errors.push(this.addCustomError(text));

  2601	    }
  2602	  }

  2619	      this.doOnAsyncCompleted(context.fireCallback, errors);
  2620	      context.setErrorElement(this, errors);
  2621	      context.removeElement(this.id);
  2622	    };
  2623	    context.addElement(this.id);
  2624	    return this.validatorRunner.run(this);
  2625	  }
  2626	  private doOnAsyncCompleted(fireCallback: boolean, errors: Array<SurveyError>): void {

  2628	      errors.forEach(er => {

  2630	          this.errors.push(er);
  2631	        }
  2632	      });
  2633	    }
  2634	    this.validatorRunner = null;
